# OCR 免费额度

https://console.bce.baidu.com/ai-engine/ocr/overview/index

| 服务名称                       | 状态       | 可用资源（余量/总量）  | QPS 并发限制 |
| ------------------------------ | ---------- | ---------------------- | ------------ |
| 通用文字识别（标准版）         | 待开通付费 | 免费资源：1000/1000 次 | 2            |
| 通用文字识别（标准含位置版）   | 待开通付费 | 免费资源：1000/1000 次 | 2            |
| 通用文字识别（高精度版）       | 待开通付费 | 免费资源：1000/1000 次 | 2            |
| 通用文字识别（高精度含位置版） | 待开通付费 | 免费资源：500/500 次   | 2            |
| 网络图片文字识别               | 待开通付费 | 免费资源：1000/1000 次 | 2            |

## 通用文字识别（高精度版）

### 示例代码：

```java
package baidu.com;

import okhttp3.*;
import org.json.JSONObject;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import java.io.*;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.net.URLEncoder;


/**
 * 需要添加依赖
 * <!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/com.squareup.okhttp3/okhttp -->
 * <dependency>
 *     <groupId>com.squareup.okhttp3</groupId>
 *     <artifactId>okhttp</artifactId>
 *     <version>4.12.0</version>
 * </dependency>
 */

class Sample {
    public static final String API_KEY = "nzGHDeN4xeCRUZ1bcP9e6IRS";
    public static final String SECRET_KEY = "qCdOvBFyEspvK8flT5T0BGLvspD5RQAf";

    public static final OkHttpClient HTTP_CLIENT = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder().readTimeout(300, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build();

        Request request = new Request.Builder()
            .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/rest/2.0/ocr/v1/accurate_basic?access_token=" + getAccessToken())
            .method("POST", body)
            .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
            .addHeader("Accept", "application/json")
            .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        System.out.println(response.body().string());

    }

    /**
     * 获取文件base64编码
     *
     * @param path      文件路径
     * @param urlEncode 如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,传true
     * @return base64编码信息，不带文件头
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getFileContentAsBase64(String path, boolean urlEncode) throws IOException {
        byte[] b = Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get(path));
        String base64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(b);
        if (urlEncode) {
            base64 = URLEncoder.encode(base64, "utf-8");
        }
        return base64;
    }


    /**
     * 从用户的AK，SK生成鉴权签名（Access Token）
     *
     * @return 鉴权签名（Access Token）
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getAccessToken() throws IOException {
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "grant_type=client_credentials&client_id=" + API_KEY
                + "&client_secret=" + SECRET_KEY);
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
                .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/oauth/2.0/token")
                .method("POST", body)
                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
                .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        return new JSONObject(response.body().string()).getString("access_token");
    }

}
```

## 通用文字识别（高精度含位置版）

### 示例代码：

```java
package baidu.com;

import okhttp3.*;
import org.json.JSONObject;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import java.io.*;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.net.URLEncoder;


/**
 * 需要添加依赖
 * <!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/com.squareup.okhttp3/okhttp -->
 * <dependency>
 *     <groupId>com.squareup.okhttp3</groupId>
 *     <artifactId>okhttp</artifactId>
 *     <version>4.12.0</version>
 * </dependency>
 */

class Sample {
    public static final String API_KEY = "nzGHDeN4xeCRUZ1bcP9e6IRS";
    public static final String SECRET_KEY = "qCdOvBFyEspvK8flT5T0BGLvspD5RQAf";

    public static final OkHttpClient HTTP_CLIENT = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder().readTimeout(300, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build();

    public static void main(String []args) throws IOException{
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        // image 可以通过 getFileContentAsBase64("C:\fakepath\output_left.jpg") 方法获取,如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,第二个参数传true
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "image=%2F9j%2F4AAQSkZJRgABAgAAAQABAAD%2F2wBDAAgGBgcGBQgHBwcJCQgKDBQNDAsLDBkSEw8UHRofHh0aHBwgJC4nICIsIxwcKDcpLDAxNDQ0Hyc5PTgyPC4zNDL%2F2wBDAQkJCQwLDBgNDRgyIRwhMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjIyMjL%2FwAARCATIAUwDASIAAhEBAxEB%2F8QAHwAAAQUBAQEBAQEAAAAAAAAAAAECAwQFBgcICQoL%2F8QAtRAAAgEDAwIEAwUFBAQAAAF9AQIDAAQRBRIhMUEGE1FhByJxFDKBkaEII0KxwRVS0fAkM2JyggkKFhcYGRolJicoKSo0NTY3ODk6Q0RFRkdISUpTVFVWV1hZWmNkZWZnaGlqc3R1dnd4eXqDhIWGh4iJipKTlJWWl5iZmqKjpKWmp6ipqrKztLW2t7i5usLDxMXGx8jJytLT1NXW19jZ2uHi4%2BTl5ufo6erx8vP09fb3%2BPn6%2F8QAHwEAAwEBAQEBAQEBAQAAAAAAAAECAwQFBgcICQoL%2F8QAtREAAgECBAQDBAcFBAQAAQJ3AAECAxEEBSExBhJBUQdhcRMiMoEIFEKRobHBCSMzUvAVYnLRChYkNOEl8RcYGRomJygpKjU2Nzg5OkNERUZHSElKU1RVVldYWVpjZGVmZ2hpanN0dXZ3eHl6goOEhYaHiImKkpOUlZaXmJmaoqOkpaanqKmqsrO0tba3uLm6wsPExcbHyMnK0tPU1dbX2Nna4uPk5ebn6Onq8vP09fb3%2BPn6%2F9oADAMBAAIRAxEAPwD2TTPD1nDao93Ak87gF%2FMG5V9gDxV7%2Bx9M%2FwCgdaf9%2BF%2Fwq7RTbbEopFL%2Bx9M%2F6B1p%2FwB%2BF%2Fwo%2FsfTP%2Bgdaf8Afhf8KzIfFRuo%2FOtNC1a4gYkJNGkQVwDjIzIDjjuBUTeNtOWOKQWt6yMnmTFY1%2F0dfMMfz%2FN%2FeVh8u77p9sl2FkbH9j6Z%2FwBA60%2F78L%2FhR%2FY%2Bmf8AQOs%2F%2B%2FC%2F4Vdoouwsil%2FY%2Bmf9A6z%2FAO%2FC%2FwCFH9j6Z%2F0DrP8A78L%2FAIVdoouwsil%2FY%2Bmf9A6z%2FwC%2FC%2F4Uf2Ppn%2FQOs%2F8Avwv%2BFXaKLsLIpf2Ppn%2FQOs%2F%2B%2FC%2F4Uf2Ppf8A0DbP%2Fvwv%2BFXaKLsLIpf2Ppf%2FAEDbP%2Fvwv%2BFH9j6X%2FwBA2z%2F78L%2FhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP8A78L%2FAIUf2Npf%2FQNs%2FwDvwv8AhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP%2FAL8L%2FhR%2FY2l%2F9A2z%2FwC%2FC%2F4Vdoouwsil%2FY2l%2FwDQNs%2F%2B%2FC%2F4Uf2Npf8A0DbP%2Fvwv%2BFXaKLsLIpf2Npf%2FAEDbP%2Fvwv%2BFH9jaX%2FwBA2z%2F78L%2FhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP8A78L%2FAIUf2Npf%2FQNs%2FwDvwv8AhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP%2FAL8L%2FhR%2FY2l%2F9A2z%2FwC%2FC%2F4Vdoouwsil%2FY2l%2FwDQNs%2F%2B%2FC%2F4Uf2Npf8A0DbP%2Fvwv%2BFXaKLsLIpf2Npf%2FAEDbP%2Fvwv%2BFH9jaX%2FwBA2z%2F78L%2FhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP8A78L%2FAIUf2Npf%2FQNs%2FwDvwv8AhV2ii7CyKX9jaX%2F0DbP%2FAL8L%2FhR%2FY2l%2F9A2z%2FwC%2FC%2F4Vdoouwsil%2FY2l%2FwDQNs%2F%2B%2FC%2F4Uf2Npf8A0DbP%2Fvwv%2BFXaoanrek6KsbarqllYLKSIzdXCRByOuNxGa         Request request = new Request.Builder()
            .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/rest/2.0/ocr/v1/accurate?access_token=" + getAccessToken())
            .method("POST", body)
            .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
            .addHeader("Accept", "application/json")
            .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        System.out.println(response.body().string());

    }

    /**
     * 获取文件base64编码
     *
     * @param path      文件路径
     * @param urlEncode 如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,传true
     * @return base64编码信息，不带文件头
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getFileContentAsBase64(String path, boolean urlEncode) throws IOException {
        byte[] b = Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get(path));
        String base64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(b);
        if (urlEncode) {
            base64 = URLEncoder.encode(base64, "utf-8");
        }
        return base64;
    }


    /**
     * 从用户的AK，SK生成鉴权签名（Access Token）
     *
     * @return 鉴权签名（Access Token）
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getAccessToken() throws IOException {
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "grant_type=client_credentials&client_id=" + API_KEY
                + "&client_secret=" + SECRET_KEY);
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
                .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/oauth/2.0/token")
                .method("POST", body)
                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
                .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        return new JSONObject(response.body().string()).getString("access_token");
    }

}
```

## 通用文字识别（标准版）

### 示例代码：

```java
package baidu.com;

import okhttp3.*;
import org.json.JSONObject;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import java.io.*;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.net.URLEncoder;


/**
 * 需要添加依赖
 * <!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/com.squareup.okhttp3/okhttp -->
 * <dependency>
 *     <groupId>com.squareup.okhttp3</groupId>
 *     <artifactId>okhttp</artifactId>
 *     <version>4.12.0</version>
 * </dependency>
 */

class Sample {
    public static final String API_KEY = "nzGHDeN4xeCRUZ1bcP9e6IRS";
    public static final String SECRET_KEY = "qCdOvBFyEspvK8flT5T0BGLvspD5RQAf";

    public static final OkHttpClient HTTP_CLIENT = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder().readTimeout(300, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build();

    public static void main(String []args) throws IOException{
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        // image 可以通过 getFileContentAsBase64("C:\fakepath\output_left.jpg") 方法获取,如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,第二个参数传true
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, %2FTVf8KvhiCCOoqcyqx3bypxzik5TXVjUIdjFl8F2vlk6Trt%2FwDaQMql9h0f24xj61h28zyB0mjMc8TGOWM%2FwsOtdrJIC6srcjrXGXTf8VLqo9XRvxI%2F%2BtV05SejInFR2JM0ZpuaM1oQOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADN1G6o80ZqhEm6jdUeaM0ASbqv%2BGGxp10P%2BnuT%2BdZmau%2BHGxY3P%2FX1J%2FOoqfCVD4jf3Ubqg30b6xN7E5cAZJrX8P8AhvUPEsw8jMFmDh7lxx9F9TSeDdL0rWtWZNVutqxtiK1%2B6Jj7t%2FSvZ4kht4UihjEcaDCqowAKmU1EynJ7IzdP8P2Hh%2ByFtYxbQRmSQ8vIfVj3%2FpWH4m8NrrzWzG8a2NuWIKxh85x7j0rrLi4VkHByKy551GeDUSn710RFM8o%2FsW4h1o6bf3QthjMc4j3LJzx9K1j4MIbb%2FbI3dceSM%2Fzrd8SRWN7pkgumMZT5o5Mcq3auT8N6jcXOvRPclj%2FonykjBIDED6%2FWq521dGqXcyGzFNLCzBjE5TcBjOKN1R3D%2FwDEwvP%2BuzfzqPfVlJaFkPyK5O5bPiXVD%2F1y%2Fka6QPzXLzn%2FAIqLUj7R%2FwAjWlPdkVNkT5ozUeaM1qZEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNAEmaM1HmjNADc0ZpmaM0CH5ozTM0ZoAfmrXh9sWVz%2FANfMn86pZq3oH%2FHjcf8AXzJ%2FOoqfCXT%2BI199G%2BmYb0pDkdRWB0CN5iSebC2Gzkj1rvvCnxEaMLZ6qzOg4Ep%2B8n19RXBZqOSMOQwO1x0YUNKSsyXG59CG4iuIVlhkWSNxlWU5BFYWrataaaE%2B1SbPMzt4JzivMtA8V3uiSiF23QMeYyflPuPQ1f8AGmsQ6tDpj2sxXJk3r3Xgday9nZ2JSsLd65bazrGy5laOxg%2BbYASX%2BtaZ1jRBdC6UEThBGGCnhB0XHpXACHaPkkdSepB60eW%2F%2FPeT860cVsVYuSyiS8uZFOVaViKbvqFBsXGSe5Jp%2BGPY1RSJA3Irm5z%2FAMVBqP0j%2Fka6EAgjI71zk5%2F4n%2BofSP8Aka0pbsyq7ImzRmmZozWpiPzRmmZozQA%2FNGaZmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmigB2aM02igB2aM02jNADs0ZpuaM0ANzRmm0UAOzRmm0UAOzVnw7Krw3cGcOtw5Hvk1UqiXl0%2B6edFdoZDuJTqp%2FwpSV1YcXyu52mTtAIcEelG0tHyDketcp%2FwkqD%2FAJfWHsVP%2BFH%2FAAksf%2FP8f%2B%2BT%2FhWPs5djb2ke502xv7p%2FKjY390%2FlXM%2F8JKn%2FAD%2FH%2Fvk%2F4Uf8JKn%2FAD%2FH%2Fvk%2F4Uezl2D2se50rRF1wyEj6VGtvKHXJYomdoI55rnv%2BElT%2Fn%2BP%2FfJ%2Fwo%2F4SVP%2Bf4%2F98n%2FCnyS7B7SPc6bY390%2FlS7G%2Fun8q5j%2FAISVP%2Bf4%2FwDfJ%2Fwo%2FwCElT%2Fn%2BP8A3yf8KXs5dg9rHudQkbFhkECpGzuxhsD0rk%2F%2BEmT%2FAJ%2Fj%2FwB8n%2FCj%2FhJk%2FwCf4%2F8AfJ%2Fwp%2Bzl2D2ke51ZyzAkFVHXNcqZhPrWoSL93KKD9Aajl1%2Fz02RyyTseiqp%2FWksoXhjZpCPMkbc2O3tVwi1qzOpNSskW80ZpuaM1ZA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmigB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igBuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSZozQAtFJRQAtFJRQAgwyhl5U9DRRRW%2BJpqnVcY7GdKTlBNhRRRWBoFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFAH%2F9k%3D&url=https%3A%2F%2Fbaidu-ai.bj.bcebos.com%2Focr%2Fgeneral.png&detect_direction=false&detect_language=false&paragraph=false&probability=false");
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
            .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/rest/2.0/ocr/v1/general_basic?access_token=" + getAccessToken())
            .method("POST", body)
            .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
            .addHeader("Accept", "application/json")
            .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        System.out.println(response.body().string());

    }

    /**
     * 获取文件base64编码
     *
     * @param path      文件路径
     * @param urlEncode 如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,传true
     * @return base64编码信息，不带文件头
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getFileContentAsBase64(String path, boolean urlEncode) throws IOException {
        byte[] b = Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get(path));
        String base64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(b);
        if (urlEncode) {
            base64 = URLEncoder.encode(base64, "utf-8");
        }
        return base64;
    }


    /**
     * 从用户的AK，SK生成鉴权签名（Access Token）
     *
     * @return 鉴权签名（Access Token）
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getAccessToken() throws IOException {
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "grant_type=client_credentials&client_id=" + API_KEY
                + "&client_secret=" + SECRET_KEY);
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
                .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/oauth/2.0/token")
                .method("POST", body)
                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
                .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        return new JSONObject(response.body().string()).getString("access_token");
    }

}
```

## 通用文字识别（标准含位置版）

### 示例代码：

```java
package baidu.com;

import okhttp3.*;
import org.json.JSONObject;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import java.io.*;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.net.URLEncoder;


/**
 * 需要添加依赖
 * <!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/com.squareup.okhttp3/okhttp -->
 * <dependency>
 *     <groupId>com.squareup.okhttp3</groupId>
 *     <artifactId>okhttp</artifactId>
 *     <version>4.12.0</version>
 * </dependency>
 */

class Sample {
    public static final String API_KEY = "nzGHDeN4xeCRUZ1bcP9e6IRS";
    public static final String SECRET_KEY = "qCdOvBFyEspvK8flT5T0BGLvspD5RQAf";

    public static final OkHttpClient HTTP_CLIENT = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder().readTimeout(300, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build();

    public static void main(String []args) throws IOException{
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        // image 可以通过 getFileContentAsBase64("C:\fakepath\output_left.jpg") 方法获取,如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,第二个参数传true

1ZA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmigB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igBuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSZozQAtFJRQAtFJRQAgwyhl5U9DRRRW%2BJpqnVcY7GdKTlBNhRRRWBoFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFAH%2F9k%3D&url=https%3A%2F%2Fbaidu-ai.bj.bcebos.com%2Focr%2Fgeneral.png&detect_direction=false&detect_language=false&vertexes_location=false&paragraph=false&probability=false");
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
            .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/rest/2.0/ocr/v1/general?access_token=" + getAccessToken())
            .method("POST", body)
            .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
            .addHeader("Accept", "application/json")
            .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        System.out.println(response.body().string());

    }

    /**
     * 获取文件base64编码
     *
     * @param path      文件路径
     * @param urlEncode 如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,传true
     * @return base64编码信息，不带文件头
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getFileContentAsBase64(String path, boolean urlEncode) throws IOException {
        byte[] b = Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get(path));
        String base64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(b);
        if (urlEncode) {
            base64 = URLEncoder.encode(base64, "utf-8");
        }
        return base64;
    }


    /**
     * 从用户的AK，SK生成鉴权签名（Access Token）
     *
     * @return 鉴权签名（Access Token）
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getAccessToken() throws IOException {
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "grant_type=client_credentials&client_id=" + API_KEY
                + "&client_secret=" + SECRET_KEY);
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
                .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/oauth/2.0/token")
                .method("POST", body)
                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
                .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        return new JSONObject(response.body().string()).getString("access_token");
    }

}
```

## 网络图片文字识别

### 示例代码：

```java
package baidu.com;

import okhttp3.*;
import org.json.JSONObject;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import java.io.*;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.net.URLEncoder;


/**
 * 需要添加依赖
 * <!-- https://mvnrepository.com/artifact/com.squareup.okhttp3/okhttp -->
 * <dependency>
 *     <groupId>com.squareup.okhttp3</groupId>
 *     <artifactId>okhttp</artifactId>
 *     <version>4.12.0</version>
 * </dependency>
 */

class Sample {
    public static final String API_KEY = "nzGHDeN4xeCRUZ1bcP9e6IRS";
    public static final String SECRET_KEY = "qCdOvBFyEspvK8flT5T0BGLvspD5RQAf";

    public static final OkHttpClient HTTP_CLIENT = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder().readTimeout(300, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build();

    public static void main(String []args) throws IOException{
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        // image 可以通过 getFileContentAsBase64("C:\fakepath\output_left.jpg") 方法获取,如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,第二个参数传true

1ZA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmjNADs0ZpuaM0AOzRmm5ozQA7NGabmigB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igB2aM02igBuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALmjNJRQAuaM0lFAC5ozSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSUUALRSZozQAtFJRQAtFJRQAgwyhl5U9DRRRW%2BJpqnVcY7GdKTlBNhRRRWBoFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFABRRRQAUUUUAFFFFAH%2F9k%3D&url=https%3A%2F%2Fbaidu-ai.bj.bcebos.com%2Focr%2Fwebimage.jpeg&detect_language=false&detect_direction=false");
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
            .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/rest/2.0/ocr/v1/webimage?access_token=" + getAccessToken())
            .method("POST", body)
            .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
            .addHeader("Accept", "application/json")
            .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        System.out.println(response.body().string());

    }

    /**
     * 获取文件base64编码
     *
     * @param path      文件路径
     * @param urlEncode 如果Content-Type是application/x-www-form-urlencoded时,传true
     * @return base64编码信息，不带文件头
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getFileContentAsBase64(String path, boolean urlEncode) throws IOException {
        byte[] b = Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get(path));
        String base64 = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(b);
        if (urlEncode) {
            base64 = URLEncoder.encode(base64, "utf-8");
        }
        return base64;
    }


    /**
     * 从用户的AK，SK生成鉴权签名（Access Token）
     *
     * @return 鉴权签名（Access Token）
     * @throws IOException IO异常
     */
    static String getAccessToken() throws IOException {
        MediaType mediaType = MediaType.parse("application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
        RequestBody body = RequestBody.create(mediaType, "grant_type=client_credentials&client_id=" + API_KEY
                + "&client_secret=" + SECRET_KEY);
        Request request = new Request.Builder()
                .url("https://aip.baidubce.com/oauth/2.0/token")
                .method("POST", body)
                .addHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded")
                .build();
        Response response = HTTP_CLIENT.newCall(request).execute();
        return new JSONObject(response.body().string()).getString("access_token");
    }

}
```
